+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+// Obtiene facturas de un cliente con sus pagos
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+export async function getClientInvoicesAction(
+  clientId: string,
+  wispId: string
+) {
+  try {
+    const supabase = await verifyWisp(wispId)
+
+    const { data: client, error: clientErr } = await supabase
+      .from('isp_clients')
+      .select('id')
+      .eq('id', clientId)
+      .eq('wisp_id', wispId)
+      .single()
+
+    if (clientErr || !client) {
+      throw new Error('Cliente no encontrado o sin permisos')
+    }
+
+    const { data, error } = await supabase
+      .from('client_invoices')
+      .select(`
+        id,
+        amount,
+        status,
+        due_date,
+        paid_at,
+        created_at,
+        client_payments (
+          id,
+          amount_paid,
+          payment_method,
+          paid_at,
+          notes,
+          source,
+          receipt_url
+        )
+      `)
+      .eq('client_id', clientId)
+      .eq('wisp_id', wispId)
+      .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
+
+    if (error) throw error
+    return { success: true, data: data || [] }
+  } catch (error: any) {
+    return { success: false, error: error.message }
+  }
+}
+
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+// Registra un pago manual para un cliente
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+export async function registerPaymentAction(
+  clientId: string,
+  wispId: string,
+  payment: {
+    amount: number
+    payment_method: 'efectivo' | 'transferencia' | 'otro'
+    paid_at: string
+    notes?: string
+  }
+) {
+  try {
+    const supabase = await verifyWisp(wispId)
+
+    const { data: client, error: clientErr } = await supabase
+      .from('isp_clients')
+      .select('id')
+      .eq('id', clientId)
+      .eq('wisp_id', wispId)
+      .single()
+
+    if (clientErr || !client) {
+      throw new Error('Cliente no encontrado o sin permisos')
+    }
+
+    // Buscar factura pendiente existente
+    let invoiceId: string
+
+    const { data: pending } = await supabase
+      .from('client_invoices')
+      .select('id')
+      .eq('client_id', clientId)
+      .eq('wisp_id', wispId)
+      .eq('status', 'pending')
+      .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
+      .limit(1)
+      .maybeSingle()
+
+    if (pending) {
+      invoiceId = pending.id
+      await supabase
+        .from('client_invoices')
+        .update({
+          status: 'paid',
+          paid_at: payment.paid_at,
+          updated_at: new Date().toISOString()
+        })
+        .eq('id', invoiceId)
+        .eq('wisp_id', wispId)
+    } else {
+      const { data: newInvoice, error: invoiceErr } = await supabase
+        .from('client_invoices')
+        .insert({
+          wisp_id: wispId,
+          client_id: clientId,
+          amount: payment.amount,
+          status: 'paid',
+          paid_at: payment.paid_at,
+        })
+        .select('id')
+        .single()
+
+      if (invoiceErr || !newInvoice) {
+        throw new Error('Error al crear factura')
+      }
+      invoiceId = newInvoice.id
+    }
+
+    const { error: paymentErr } = await supabase
+      .from('client_payments')
+      .insert({
+        invoice_id: invoiceId,
+        amount_paid: payment.amount,
+        payment_method: payment.payment_method,
+        paid_at: payment.paid_at,
+        notes: payment.notes || null,
+        source: 'manual',
+        receipt_url: null
+      })
+
+    if (paymentErr) throw paymentErr
+
+    revalidatePath('/dashboard/clientes')
+    return { success: true }
+  } catch (error: any) {
+    return { success: false, error: error.message }
+  }
+}
